Canadian Expeditionary<br>
Force<br>
60th BATTALION<br>
(and Reinforcing Draft)<br>

Officers and Men.<br>
EMBARKATION<br>
(Port: Montreal.<br>
Ship: S.S. 11 Scandinavian."<br>

10m-6-lS.<br>
H.Q. 593-2-29.<br>
Reinforcing Draft<br>
Port: Montreal.<br>
Ship: S.S. "Scandinavian."<br>
Date: August 27th, 1915.
